<user>101299775466215223698<//user><Rate>5</Rate><Response>None<//Response><Time>1620007968608<//Time><Review>Best Experience Ever!

Found this place one day as I was leaving town on a Sunday. They were the only place open on a Sunday so I stopped by to get a flat fixed and also asked the mechanic to check my fluids before I embark on my road trip. Nothing but positivity and great work. As my vehicle was finished, the Boss came out and spoke to me about my tires and how far my trip was going to be. She said I needed new tires and that my vehicle would get better MPG  and overall would ride smoother with these new tires. I was sold on them!

Long story short, I told her I'd be back in a few weeks and that I'd love to get all four tires. Ended up getting the Falken Wildpeak AT Trail and I absolutely love them! I got them mounted and balanced and even an alignment. Ever since that day, I've been coming here ever since. Amazing work, and great customer service.

I commute often down to Southern California and stop by Pacific Tire every time!

< Review>
I came here out of desperation. I was on my way to LA for a trip for a concert. My dumb butt forgot to change one of the tires before we left Arizona. Luckily our bad tire made it to civilization when it ended up shredded. To make a long story short, we ended up getting help from roadside assistance who put my spare on and urged me to get to a tire shop immediately. I was so scared and had no idea where I was or who to trust. I ended up at this little place. They got me in and gave me a brand new tire for super cheap in less than 15 minutes when I was really pressed for time and concerned about money. They were so kind and fluent in English and Spanish, which I have major respect for since I only speak English. They worked fast and after a very stressful couple of hours trying to get roadside assistance in an unfamiliar area, made me feel hopeful and excited about my trip again. I‚Äôm so glad I came to this shop, they are trustworthy and fast. They made me feel so relieved when I had been sobbing that my trip was ruined just before this. I can never thank them enough for what they did for me, but I hope this business thrives and continues for years to come. They deserve it.< /Review>

<text>Was quoted $30 to get two tires repaired. I asked if that included balancing and he said it did.  One tire was not repairable and he offered to sell a used tire for $50 which I agreed.

I watched them repair my other tire and while they were in process of reinstalling onto car I asked about rebalancing.  The guy said "this was the repaired tire," like repaired tires don't need rebalancing.  Any reputable tire store always rebalances the wheel after the tire has been removed and reinstalled. He then offered to rebalance for an extra $5. Rather than argue over $5, I agreed.  What else can go wrong?

Well, after rebalancing the wheel he proceeded to install on car and tighten the lug nuts with his impact wrench.  Now, it's ok to remove lug nuts with an impact wrench (they're fast), and ok to install with impact wrench and lighty torque the nuts, but final torque should always be applied with a calibrated hand torque wrench as all reputable tire stores do.   Over-torquing with an impact wrench can damage threads or warp brake rotors, and under-torquing can cause lug nuts and wheels to fall off.  I asked if he was going to apply final torque with a torque wrench and he looked at me like "hey my job's done."  After further pushing I found out the shop did not even own a torque wrench!    And this is a place that also advertises such services as brakes, differential repairs and more.. All requiring specific torque values of components for proper repair.  Unbelievable!!< /text><Gmap_id>0x80c32de095233f6d:0x68120d99f349fc67< /Gmap_id><Pics>None<//Pics></record></dataset><record>

My husband and I dropped in at CrossFit Santa Monica during our recent trip to the west coast. We attended the "Kettle Bell Hell" class. We were welcomed by friendly staff and members. < text>
When I heard that a new box had opened in my neighborhood, I was super psyched.  Then I heard it was run by Navy SEALs and I was, obviously, a lottle nervous.  But all my fears were alleviated after the first workout.  It was hard (it's CrossFit, duh), but there wasn't a brass bell hanging anywhere.  Nobody was washing out.  (That is the extent of my Navy SEAL lingo, so I'll move on.)

The coaches are great!  I've mostly worked with Coach Michael who is AWESOME, but the other coaches (Carter and Kaj) are fabulous as well.  My level of CrossFit has greatly improved since I started here.  They take the time to help with your form which is important for someone like me - over 40 and relatively new to the game.  I won't recover from an injury as quickly as the spring chickens, so I need to get it right.  BIG points for that!

And the place is clean and organized.  Maybe I'm the only person who really takes note when I see something like clean bathrooms, but they're so clean that I was taken aback.  ABACK!  Plus, towels for your sweaty, sweaty face.  It's glorious.< /text>

<user>100521075691411792722<//user>< text>
Crossfit Santa Monica is AMAZING. I have been doing crossfit for about a year now back on the east coast at school and I am out here for the summer with my sister. We were trying to find a good box to workout at and came across Crossfit Santa Monica. Throughout all of the spring, we were messaging back and forth to Carter, one of the owners, who could not have been more welcoming and excited for our arrival.  Not only is all the equipment new and top of the line but facility is beyond my expectation. The showers are amazing with shampoo/conditioner, fresh towels, new razors and clean space...something that I do not take for granted when I have to get ready for work after a 6:30 am workout.

The coaches are awesome and supportive! We always go through the workout before hand with the movements so that everyone knows what they're doing and so no one gets hurt. Even as an experienced crossfitter, it's always good to go over the movements. And during the workout everyone goes at their own pace and scale the workout to their level. They push you to work hard and do your best. The other owner, Kaj, is a bundle of joy and the nicest guy ever. Always making everyone laugh and have a good time to forget about how hard a workout might be. Overall, such a great box with great amenities, free parking, and awesome people!< /text>

<Text>After my husband and I moved to Santa Monica, one of our first to-do items was to find our new crossfit box.  Having just moved from the east coast, we were anxious to find a box where we would fit in and could get a great work out.  I'm happy to say that Crossfit Santa Monica has more than met those expectations.

First comes first--location.  You can't beat the prime real estate on Main St. just minutes from the beach where WODs are often held, which is just a huge bonus.  Next, the programming is spot on.  There is a nice mix between killer burners and short AMRAPS, plus they focus on skill work, like toes-to-bar and double unders, which I've found that many other gyms often overlook.  Finally and most importantly, the coaches are really great in many ways.  They teach the technique of all the movements very well and you can tell they generally care about helping ALL the athletes, not just the elite competitors.

All in all, Crossfit Santa Monica is a fantastic box that has made our move to a new city that much easier.  Now that we have a box as good as CFSM, we are happy to call Santa Monica home.<//Text></record>

< Text>
I first visited CrossFit Santa Monica in late-March and have been hooked ever since.

Let's face it, CrossFit looks intimidating. Ripped men and women, heavy weights, quick times and all that WOD lingo... It can be overwhelming for a newbie. CFSM made me feel right at home. I almost puked after my first workout, but undeterred I kept at it, and am glad I did.

The instructors are knowledgable, members are friendly and the location is prime time. If you're lucky, you'll even get a beach workout. What I like most about CFSM is the atmosphere. Other boxes overemphasize time and weight, which IMO is a total deterrent. Let's face it, I'm at CFSM for a good workout and some motivation. I'm not trying to compete, and there's no way I'm going to hang clean 110 pounds. The encouragement I get from staff and members pushes me to try harder and lift more. Members stay until everyone completes the WOD. CFSM's camaraderie is awesome.

After a few months at CFSM I feel stronger and look leaner, but I'm not the only one who notices. Between pool parties and beach days, I've received countless comments on my physique and what I do to stay fit. I'm like, "Oh, CrossFit Santa Monica, they're the best." For reals though, I haven't felt this good about my body since competitive dance team days almost ten years ago.

If you're looking to give CrossFit a try, look no further than this box. It blows the competition out of the Pacific.< /Text>

< Review>
Encore academy is a fanatastic school ! I am new to the world of aviation and have always wanted to fly. Before coming to Encore, I wasn‚Äôt exactly sure if this was something I wanted to do for fun or for my career. I booked a  consultation with the lovely girl in the friend desk who was super helpful and attentive and helped get me an appointment right away. I met with Alex and he was very thorough with all the different packages they offer and patient with all my questions! I started my training here and I absolutely love it! The staff here makes you feel like family and the instructors are all so professional. I honestly feel like out of all the other schools I looked into, Encore was hands down the most versatile and professional around. I definitely made the right decision by coming here. I would definitely recommend this school to anyone who wants to get any of their ratings. They offer career packages as well for those who want to become a pilot for airline. Thank you encore for making this experience an incredible one so far!<//Review>

<user>118126599743645791978</user><user_name>Michael Rubestein< /user_name>< time>

<Text>If you what first class service you need to checkout Encore Flight.

I am current student at Encore, I started flying here about a six months ago. I signed up the complete package they offer, I am going to get my Private Pilot, Instrument and Multi engine ratings. The training has been a lot fun so far, I tried all their aircraft and I decided on the Diamond.

The main advantage for me has been the ability to cross train between flight simulators and the aircraft. With all their simulators, I usually practice the maneuvers in the sims before I get to try them in the real aircraft. <review>Brief background about myself. I am currently a full time pharmacy school student at USC and I have a part time job. I recently turned 25 and I have two years left in my pharmD program. I decided that I wanted to get a private pilot license as a hobby. The idea of flying is just so cool and it is a very unique skill to have. For anyone out there who is interested in getting their private pilot license hopefully you will find this review to be helpful for you. I will provide an overview of my experience in getting my private pilot license at Encore and what I liked and what I would have done differently if I had to get my license all over again.

First and foremost, Encore is a legit flying school. From what I can tell, the majority of Encore's instructors are nice people and have very useful information when it comes to instructing students and helping students become competent and comfortable to fly. They have plenty of planes to fly with and there was never really an issue when scheduling planes for my flying lesson. If one plane was under scheduled maintenance there was always another plane that my instructor and I could take up instead. Encore always has certified airplane mechanics on staff to make sure the planes are safe and compliant under regulation. Shirley, who works at the front and handles literally everything is beyond competent. Alex is the owner of Encore and he is a nice guy. If I had to get my license again I would still go with encore, but here are some things I noticed and here is what I would have done differently.

I personally underestimated this process. I thought that because I am an athletic guy and I got into a doctorate program so I should be able to get good at flying really quick. That wasn't quite the case. I passed my private pilot checkride (test) around the 70 hour mark. I passed first try but it definitely took longer than I had intended. There are definitely people that can finish sooner than 70 hours but just keep in mind that you may have to spend over 40 hours (the minimum legal amount) to become competent at flying the plane safely.

This brings me to my next point, if you are about to start flying, I would recommend finishing the whole process in one sitting. Be able to dedicate a few months to studying and flying and try not to take an extended hiatus. I had to take about 6 months off of flying due to school and as a result I had to relearn some things to become proficient for the checkride again so I ended up having to take more lessons and essentially pay more money. FINISH IN ONE SITTING. Don't fly for one month and take another month off and then come back to flying. It will save you a lot of money in the long run to have consistency in your training. Be super proactive about your training. You have to want it for yourself.

Finally, you may end up spending more money than you initially intended to. You may need over 40 hours to become comfortable enough with flying a plane. Buying extra study materials cost money. Decent flying headsets can cost 300 and up. The final checkride costs about $800. Insurance will cost a couple hundred dollars. Essentially, whatever you think flying is going to cost, add a couple thousand or more to that amount. Flying is an expensive hobby, there's no doubt about that. But it can also be a lucrative career if you are trying to fly for a commercial company.

I am beyond glad I got my private pilot license. I am not exaggerating when I say that it has been one of the most rewarding experiences of my life. Since I got my license, I have flown my girlfriend over Malibu. It was just such a sick experience to be able to fly passengers myself. I would encourage everyone to fly. If you want to become a pilot, Encore will take you to where you need to be.<//review><Rating>5< /Rating>< user_id>

< Text>
I do not recommend Encore Flight Academy for flight training.
On Sept 13, 2017, I put down a $5000 block payment for flight instruction for a multi-engine add-on.  I have a commercial instrument rating.  Encore's requirement was that any balance left in the account would be refunded back to me if and when I completed the training with them (i.e. passed the check ride).  My requirement was that Encore would provide me as much flight instruction by Sept 28, when I was permanently moving from Los Angeles to the Bay Area.  Alex A. the owner and I agreed to those terms.  His words were "we can do our part; it's all up to you"

At my behest, Alex C, my assigned instructor sat down with me to create a training plan and to schedule a weeks worth of flights on the calendar.  Unfortunately, all of the scheduled flights were canceled the day of or the day prior.  The first was due to ceilings being too low, the second due to a plane missing in the hands of the mechanic who was supposed to have it ready by my schedule flight, and the remainder due to pop-up checkrides for other trainees.  In the end, I was not able to log any flight time.

I asked my instructor Alex C. if it would be reasonable to ask for a refund as I had done my best to proactively schedule as many flights as possible.  He instructed me to talk to the owner, Alex A. in-person the very next day.  Unfortunately, the admin called me the very next morning to cancel my appointment with Alex A. because of a pop up emergency.  When I asked to reschedule, she insisted I call him instead.  I was able to reach him by phone  on my first try.  On this call, I politely requested he consider the possibility of a refund and that he would be in the right to exclude from the refund whatever service charges he might have incurred on those transactions.  He said he would look into it and call me back in 2 days.  Unfortunately, I have not heard back from him since, and my repeated calls to his admin at the office and his cell now go unanswered.  I have asked my instructor Alex C. help in getting a hold of Alex A., but this is to no avail either, as he is slow to respond and claims he has not been able to do so either.  I have strong reasons to believe their avoidance is deliberate, considering that for my very first visit, I was able to schedule an in-person visit with Alex A. with an impromptu phone call a mere 30 minutes in advance.

I don't recommend Encore because of their avoidance of customers who no longer present a revenue opportunity for them, and for their lack of values and ethics.

As of now, I have $5000 in an account with them that I am not able to use nor reclaim.<//Text>

Like the previous reviewers, I want to warn other potential students / renters about this place. I went there about 2 years ago, to rent a Piper PA-28 for a few days.

As a side note: This was the second plane we used, after they couldn‚Äôt find the key for the one they originally wanted to use. Great.
I was originally planning to make a longer cross country flight every day, but ended up with only one single cross country flight and a few shorter flights, mainly due to technical issues. On top of that, the management was pretty unorganized. Even though I always showed up as scheduled and on time, they always struggled to find a functioning plane. The most frustrating experience was however, when the keys for the plane were supposed to be dropped of at the FBO on the last day of my stay, which was a holiday, so that I could go flying and use up my deposit. <Text>We were on our way to Del Taco, next door. I  saw this place, and was like, let's get real Mexican food.  It looked pretty good when we walked in. I noticed there were ONLY Hispanic folks inside, eating. I find this a good sign. Lol. (Only because  all my Hispanic friends talk about how most Mexican restaurants aren't authenic, and won't go to them).

So, it was super clean inside. The staff was extremely nice! The cashier smiled, and was friendly, and even said, oh that soda is so good! (We bought a couple bottles of appple soda)

First up, I ordered the 2 beef tacos platter, which comes with beans and rice. The tacos were really good! Very crunchy. A bit skimpy on the meat. But everything tasted fresh. Lots of flavor.

I don't usually like Mexican rice, but this was really good! It was moist, and flavorful. I liked it a lot. However, my hubby didn't care for it. He thought it was bland. We both liked the beans a lot. Very tasty.

Hubby got the fajitas, without peppers. He doesn't like spicey, and they had chili flakes, and were somewhat spicey. I like spicey, so we traded. They were super good! The chicken was tender, and had a lot of flavor. The more you ate, the spicier it got. But I liked them.

We got the chips and guacamole. The chips were good. But it's not the traditional, light and fluffy ones known at Mexican restaurants. They were like you do at home. Cut up a few corn tortillas, and fry them in oil. They were a bit hard. And the guacamole was good. But nothing special.

They have a couple of TVs around. With ball games on. They have a soda fountain, and another one with Orange bang, or horchata. Or you can buy a soda in a bottle. We got Apple. Pretty good.

I liked it, but my hubby didn't. I would like to try one if the bowls. So I may go for lunch alone. Lol<//Text>< Gmap_id>
